# Firefox Content Security Policy Enforcement Audit

## Your Task

Audit the Content Security Policy (CSP) enforcement infrastructure in Firefox. Find all C++ source files in `mozilla-firefox/firefox` under `dom/security/` that implement CSP parsing, evaluation, and violation reporting. Specifically: 1. The file that defines `nsCSPParser` — the CSP directive parser. 2. The file that implements `nsCSPContext` — the main CSP context that holds policies. 3. The file that implements CSP violation reporting (`nsCSPUtils` or similar). 4. The header file that declares the `nsIContentSecurityPolicy` XPCOM interface. 5. The file under `dom/security/` that performs script-src evaluation for inline scripts. Report each file path and its primary class or function.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/firefox--871325b8` (mozilla-firefox/firefox)

54-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've completed the Firefox Content Security Policy enforcement audit. Here's a summary of what I found:

## CSP Enforcement Infrastructure Files

I've identified and documented all the key C++ source files in Firefox's `dom/security/` directory that implement CSP parsing, evaluation, and violation reporting:

### Core Components:

1. **CSP Parser** (`nsCSPParser`)
   - `dom/security/nsCSPParser.h` (header)
   - `dom/security/nsCSPParser.cpp` (implementation)
   - Parses CSP directives from headers using tokenization

2. **CSP Context** (`nsCSPContext`)
   - `dom/security/nsCSPContext.h` (header)
   - `dom/security/nsCSPContext.cpp` (implementation)
   - Main context holding and enforcing CSP policies

3. **XPCOM Interface** (`nsIContentSecurityPolicy`)
   - `dom/interfaces/security/nsIContentSecurityPolicy.idl`
   - Defines the public CSP interface

4. **Violation Data** (`CSPViolationData`)
   - `dom/security/CSPViolationData.h/cpp`
   - Structured data for CSP violations

5. **Inline Script Evaluation**
   - `dom/security/nsCSPContext.cpp` - `GetAllowsInline()` method (line 637)
   - Evaluates script-src for inline scripts, checking nonces, hashes, and keywords

6. **Violation Reporting**
   - `ReportInlineViolation()` and `AsyncReportViolation()` in nsCSPContext.cpp
   - Generates and sends violation reports

7. **Supporting Files**
   - `dom/security/nsCSPUtils.h/cpp` - CSP utilities and constants
   - `dom/security/CSPEvalChecker.h/cpp` - Eval() enforcement

The complete findings have been written to `/workspace/answer.json` with detailed documentation of each file, symbol, and the execution chain showing how CSP policies are parsed, evaluated, and violations are reported.
